INC-SOURCE (D-T). 400-keV deuterons on tritium target.            1096000100011

DETECTOR   (MAGSP) Magnetic quadrupole triplet lens system with   1096000100014

METHOD     Charged particle energies averaged over 500-keV bins,  1096000100016
